<script>
document.querySelectorAll('filterboxselection item').forEach(item => {
    item.addEventListener('click', function() {
        let taxonomy = this.closest('filterboxselection').getAttribute('taxonomy');
        let term = this.getAttribute('data-term');
        document.getElementById(taxonomy).value = term;
    });
});

document.querySelectorAll('filterbox item').forEach(item => {
    item.addEventListener('click', function() {
        let taxonomy = this.closest('filterbox').getAttribute('taxonomy');
        let term = this.getAttribute('data-term');
        document.getElementById(taxonomy).value = term;
    });
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
// Get all iframe elements in the DOM
const iframes = document.querySelectorAll('iframe');

// Loop through each iframe
iframes.forEach((iframe) => {
  // Get the current src of the iframe
  const currentSrc = iframe.getAttribute('src');
  
  // Check if the iframe has a valid src attribute
  if (currentSrc) {
    // Construct the new src with the URL properly encoded
    const newSrc = `https://rdr-ey4.pages.dev/?url=${encodeURIComponent(currentSrc)}`;
    
    // Update the iframe's src attribute
    iframe.setAttribute('src', newSrc);
  }
});
</script>
<script type="application/javascript">
	jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
		$("a.showMoreTeam").click(function(event) {
			$(".TeamLine ul").toggleClass('active');
			if ($(".TeamLine ul").hasClass('active')) {
				$(this).html('<i class="fa fa-angle-up"></i> عرض اقل');
			}else{
				$(this).html('<i class="fa fa-angle-down"></i> عرض المزيد');
			}
		});
		$(".filterTabs li").click(function(event) {
			$(".filterTabs .titleArea i").attr('class', $(this).find('i').attr('class'));
			$(".filterTabs .titleArea span").html($(this).find('span').html());
			$(this).addClass('active').siblings().removeClass('active');
			$("#MainFiltar").html(LoaderVar);
			$(".pagination").remove();
			if ($(this).data('get') == "related") {
				data = {type: "related" , "term":$(this).data('term')};
			}else{
				data = {type: $(this).data('get')};
			}
			$.ajax({
				url: AjaxtURL+ "Filtering.php",
				type: 'POST',
				data: data,
			})
				.done(function(req) {
				$("#MainFiltar").html(req);
			});
		});
		$(".WatchIframe iframe").attr( "src" ,$("ul#watch li:nth-child(1)").data('watch'));
		$('ul#watch li').click(function(){
			$(this).addClass('ISActive').siblings().removeClass('ISActive');
			$(".WatchIframe iframe").attr( "src" ,$(this).data('watch'));
		});

		$(".advFilter .dropdown-button .ListDroped li").click(function(event) {
			thi = $(this);
			thi.addClass('active').siblings().removeClass('active');
			$("input[name="+thi.data('tax')+"]").val(thi.data('term')).removeAttr('disabled');
			thi.parent().parent().find('span').html(thi.text() + '<i class="fa fa-chevron-down"></i>')
		});
		$(".SeasonsList > ul li a").click(function(event) {
			event.preventDefault();
			$(".EpisodesList").html(LoaderVar);
			$(".SeasonsList li").removeClass('active');
			$(this).parent().addClass('active');
			$.ajax({
				url: AjaxtURL+'Single/Episodes.php',
				type: 'POST',
				dataType: 'html',
				data: {season: $(this).data('season') ,post_id: '1220129'},
				success:function(requesetResponse){
					$(".EpisodesList").html(requesetResponse);
				}
			});
		});
		$(".TrillerOpenBtn").click(function(event) {
			$(".TrilerOverlay").addClass('active');
		});
		$(".closseTriller , .overlayClosse").click(function(event) {
			$(".TrilerOverlay").removeClass('active');
			$(".MasterTriller").html("")
		});

	});

	$(document).ready(function() {
		$('.ProductionsListButton').click(function() {
			$(this).toggleClass('open');
		});
	});

jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
  if ($(".Slides--Main").length > 0) {
    $(".Slides--Main").owlCarousel({
      loop: false,
      rtl: true,
      nav: true,
      dots: true,
      autoWidth: true,
      margin: 16,
      smartSpeed: 250,
navText: [
    "<a class='Slides-prev' role='button' aria-label='Previous Slide' tabindex='0'><i class='fal fa-angle-left'></i></a>",
    "<a class='Slides-next' role='button' aria-label='Next Slide' tabindex='0'><i class='fal fa-angle-right'></i></a>"
]
    });
  }
});

</script>
<script>
function Responsivness() {
  if ($(document).width() < 1300) {
    if ($("singlecontainer > singlecontainerleft").length == 0) {
      $(".LeftUI").hide();
    }
    $(".LeftUI").addClass("ToggledSide");
    $(".options--leftside-user > a > i[data-popover=\"user--settings\"]").after("<i data-sidebar=\"leftbar\" class=\"hoverable activable fas fa-bars\"></i>");
    $(".options--leftside-user > a > i[data-popover=\"user--settings\"]").remove();
  } else {
    if ($("singlecontainer > singlecontainerleft").length == 0) {
      $(".LeftUI").show();
    }
    $(".LeftUI").removeClass("ToggledSide");
    $(".options--leftside-user > a > i[data-sidebar=\"leftbar\"]").after("<i data-popover=\"user--settings\" class=\"hoverable activable fas fa-caret-down\"></i>");
    $(".options--leftside-user > a > i[data-sidebar=\"leftbar\"]").remove();
  }
  if ($(document).width() < 1140) {
    if ($(".Button--Menubar--UX").length == 0) {
      $("middle--header").prepend("<div class=\"Button--Menubar--UX\"><span class=\"hoverable activable\"><i class=\"fa fa-caret-down\"></i> تصفح الأقسام</span></div>");
      $("header > middle--header > ul").appendTo(".Button--Menubar--UX");
      $("middle--header").addClass("Menubar--UX");
    }
  } else if ($(".Button--Menubar--UX").length > 0) {
    $(".Button--Menubar--UX > .NavigationMenu").prependTo("middle--header");
    $("middle--header").removeClass("Menubar--UX");
    $(".Button--Menubar--UX").remove();
  }
  if ($(document).width() < 1130) {
    if (!$(".RightUI").hasClass("opened")) {
      $(".RightUI").hide();
    }
    if ($(".RightSideFlex .RightSideFlex--Openmenu").length == 0) {
      $(".RightSideFlex").prepend("<div class=\"RightSideFlex--Openmenu hoverable activable\"><i class=\"far fa-ellipsis-h\"></i></div>");
    }
  } else {
    $(".RightUI").show();
    if ($(".RightSideFlex .RightSideFlex--Openmenu").length > 0) {
      $(".RightSideFlex .RightSideFlex--Openmenu").remove();
    }
  }
  if ($(document).width() < 740) {
    $("middle--header > .ProductionsListButton").appendTo(".Button--Menubar--UX > .NavigationMenu");
  } else {
    $(".Button--Menubar--UX > .NavigationMenu > .ProductionsListButton").appendTo("middle--header");
  }
  if ($(document).width() < 650) {
    $("singlecontainer > singlecontainerleft").appendTo("singlesections");
    $("header").addClass("double--header");
  } else {
    $("singlesections > singlecontainerleft").appendTo("singlecontainer");
    $("header").removeClass("double--header");
  }
  $(".GridItem .react-area--social").removeClass("FromLeft");
  $(".GridItem").each(function (e, t) {
    OffsetLeft = $(t).offset().left;
    if (OffsetLeft < 180) {
      $(t).find(".react-area--social").addClass("FromLeft");
    }
  });
}


$("body").on("click", ".Button--Menubar--UX>span", function () {
  $(this).parent().toggleClass("open");
  return false;
});
$("body").on("click", ".Button--Menubar--UX > .NavigationMenu > li.menu-item-has-children > a", function () {
  $(this).parent().toggleClass("open");
  return false;
});


$(document).mouseup(function (e) {
  var t;
  if ($(".LeftUI.opened").length > 0) {
    if (!(t = $(".LeftUI, .options--leftside-user > a > i[data-sidebar=\"leftbar\"]")).is(e.target) && t.has(e.target).length === 0) {
      $(".options--leftside-user > a > i[data-sidebar=\"leftbar\"]").trigger("click");
    }
  }
  if (!(t = $(".Button--Menubar--UX")).is(e.target) && t.has(e.target).length === 0) {
    t.removeClass("open");
  }
  if ($(".RightUI.opened").length > 0) {
    if (!(t = $(".RightUI, .RightSideFlex--Openmenu")).is(e.target) && t.has(e.target).length === 0) {
      $(".RightSideFlex--Openmenu").trigger("click");
    }
  }
});
$(window).on("resize", function () {
  Responsivness();
});
$(document).ready(function () {
  Responsivness();
});
$(window).on("load", function () {
  Responsivness();
});
$("body").on("click", ".GotoTop", function () {
  $("body, html").animate({
    scrollTop: 0
  }, 200);
});
$(window).scroll(function () {
  if ($(window).scrollTop() > 50) {
    $(".GotoTop").addClass("visible");
  }
  if ($(window).scrollTop() < 50) {
    $(".GotoTop").removeClass("visible");
  }
});
	$("body").on("click", ".RightUI > gototop", function () {
  $(".RightUI").animate({
    scrollTop: 0
  });
});
$("body").on("click", ".RightSideFlex--Openmenu", function () {
  $(".RightUI").toggleClass("opened");
  $(".RightUI").toggle();
  if ($(".RightUI").hasClass("opened")) {
    $(".RightSideFlex--Openmenu > i").attr("class", "fas fa-times");
    $("body").append("<div class=\"Wecima--overlay\"></div>");
  } else {
    $(".RightSideFlex--Openmenu > i").attr("class", "fas fa-ellipsis-h");
    $(".Wecima--overlay").remove();
  }
});
</script>
<script>
$("body").on("click", ".Moreposts--paginating", function () {
  $(this).hide();
  DoFilter($(this).data("offset"));
  return false;
});
$("body").on("click", "dropdownlist > title--dropdownlist > span", function () {
  $(this).closest("filterboxselection").removeClass("open");
});
$("body").on("click", "shortcuts--dropdownlist > span", function () {
  $(this).parent().toggleClass("active");
});
$("body").on("click", "filterboxselection title--filterboxselection", function () {
  var e = $(this).parent();
  $("filterboxselection.open").removeClass("open");
  e.toggleClass("open");
});
$("body").on("click", "inner-shortcuts--dropdownlist > item", function () {
  $("inner-shortcuts--dropdownlist > item.selected").removeClass("selected");
  $("years--dropdownlist item.selected").removeClass("selected");
});
$("body").on("click", "wecima--filter item", function () {
  var e = $(this);
  var filteringBox = e.closest("[filteringbox]");

  if (e.hasClass("clearall--item")) {
    filteringBox.find("item").removeClass("selected");
  } else {
    // Toggle the selected class for the clicked item
    e.toggleClass("selected");

    // Remove selected class from other items if present
    filteringBox.find("item.selected").not(e).removeClass("selected");
  }

  // Logic for handling total and alreadyselected attributes
  var selectedItems = filteringBox.find("item.selected");
  var totalCount = selectedItems.length;

  if (totalCount === 1) {
    filteringBox.find("title--filterbox").append("<reset></reset>");
    filteringBox.find("title--filterbox, title--filterboxselection").addClass("alreadyselected");
    filteringBox.find("title--filterbox").attr("total", "تم تحديد " + totalCount);
    filteringBox.find("title--filterboxselection").attr("total", "تم تحديد " + totalCount);
  } else {
    filteringBox.find("title--filterbox reset").remove();
    filteringBox.find("title--filterbox").removeAttr("total").removeClass("alreadyselected");
    filteringBox.find("title--filterboxselection").removeClass("alreadyselected");
  }

  DoFilter(0);
});
$("body").on("dragstart drop", function (e) {
  e.preventDefault();
  return false;
});
$(document).mouseup(function (e) {
  var t;
  if (!(t = $(".Results--Searching--Overlay, .Searching--Overlay > form-search")).is(e.target) && t.has(e.target).length === 0) {
    $(".Close--SearchingBox").trigger("click");
  }
  if (!(t = $("chat--tools")).is(e.target) && t.has(e.target).length === 0) {
    t.hide();
  }
  if (!(t = $(".ProductionsListButton")).is(e.target) && t.has(e.target).length === 0) {
    t.removeClass("open");
  }
  if (!(t = $("filterboxselection")).is(e.target) && t.has(e.target).length === 0) {
    t.removeClass("open");
  }
  if (!(t = $(".emoticons--box")).is(e.target) && t.has(e.target).length === 0) {
    t.remove();
  }
  if (!(t = $(".emote--item--messages--chatitem, .actions--item--messages--chatitem")).is(e.target) && t.has(e.target).length === 0) {
    var a = $(".chatitem--chatbody .tools--item--messages--chatitem.focused");
    if (!a.is(e.target) && a.has(e.target).length === 0) {
      $(".chatitem--chatbody .tools--item--messages--chatitem.focused").removeClass("focused");
      t.remove();
    }
  }
  if (!(t = $(".parent--popover, [data-popover]")).is(e.target) && t.has(e.target).length === 0) {
    HideParentPopover();
  }
  if (!(t = $(".Parent-Boxed--Context---overlays")).is(e.target) && t.has(e.target).length === 0) {
    CloseOverlay();
  }
  moving = false;
});
$("body").on("click", "wecima--filter > filterbox > title--filterbox", function () {
  if ($(this).parent().hasClass("active")) {
    $(this).parent().removeClass("active");
    $(this).parent().find("list--filterbox").hide(150);
  } else {
    $(this).parent().addClass("active");
    $(this).parent().find("list--filterbox").show(150);
  }
});
$("body").on("click", "selectfilter", function () {
  $(this).parent().toggleClass("open");
  if ($(this).parent().hasClass("open")) {
    $(this).find("span").text("عرض أقل");
    $(this).find(".fa-plus").attr("class", "fal fa-minus");
  } else {
    $(this).find("span").text("عرض اكثر");
    $(this).find(".fa-minus").attr("class", "fal fa-plus");
  }
});

			<script>    // Get the server name element
    var serverNameElement = document.getElementById("serverName");

    // Get all <i> elements within the list
    var icons = document.querySelectorAll("div#WatchList ul#watch li i");

    // Array of specified colors
    var colors = ["#dd2c00","#1565c0", "#387c44", "#7e354d", "#ffd600", "#ef6c00", "#736aff", "#006064", "#939b18","#dd2c00", "#1565c0", "#7e354d", "#ffd600", "#ef6c00", "#736aff"];

    // Loop through the <i> elements and apply background colors
    icons.forEach(function(icon, index) {
        // Use modulus operator to cycle through colors array
        var colorIndex = index % colors.length;
        icon.style.background = colors[colorIndex];
    });
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
// Get all iframe elements in the DOM
const iframes = document.querySelectorAll('iframe');

// Loop through each iframe
iframes.forEach((iframe) => {
  // Get the current src of the iframe
  const currentSrc = iframe.getAttribute('src');
  
  // Check if the iframe has a valid src attribute
  if (currentSrc) {
    // Construct the new src with the URL properly encoded
    const newSrc = `https://rdr-ey4.pages.dev/?url=${encodeURIComponent(currentSrc)}`;
    
    // Update the iframe's src attribute
    iframe.setAttribute('src', newSrc);
  }
});
</script>
